Rw;        case 2:            _Rh = Mh;            _Rw = Rw * Mh / Rh;        case 3:            _Rh = (Rh / Mh > Rw / Mw) ? Mh: Rh * Mw / Rw;            _Rw = (Rh / Mh > Rw / Mw) ? Rw * Mh / Rh: Mw        }        if (index != 0) {            need_resize = true        }        return [_Rw, _Rh]    }    var wh = getRightWH(_image.width, _image.height, _Mw, _Mh);    o.style.width = wh[0] + 'px';    o.style.height = wh[1] + 'px';    o.setAttribute("width",wh[0]);    o.setAttribute("height",wh[1]);    o.style.visibility = 'visible';    if (need_margin == true) {        o.style.marginTop = (Mh - parseInt(wh[1])) / 2 + 'px'    }    _image = null;    return need_resize}/*签名档加载失败处理*/function sign_change_img(img){img.src='//tb1.bdstatic.com/tb/static-itieba/img/sign_err.png';img.width=100;img.height=25;}</script><style style="text/css">.special_conf_skin{background:;}</style><div id="head"
